Merging K Sorted Lists Oracle ^99kFav53

You are given an array of k linked-lists lists, each linked-list is sorted in ascending order. ^MchfarIQ

Class Node;
    int vale
    Node next ^WI9m3zA8

slow = head
fast = head

while fast and fast.next is not null
    slow = slow.next
    fast = fast.next.next
    if slow == fast
        return True ^jGIyMKjw

Merge Sort Algorithm ^4wm311UT

dummy = Node(0)
current = dummy
while l1 and l2:
    if l1.val < l2.val
        current.next = l1
        l1 = l1.next
    else:
        current.next = l2
        l2 = l2.next
    current = current.next
# add left over
current.next = l1 or l2
return dummy.next ^ps2Db6dc

lists = []

while lists.length > 1
    ans = []
    for i in range(0, list.lenght, 2)
        list1 = lists[i]
        list2 = lists[i+1] # condition, if its available
        res = mergelist(list1, list2)
        ans.add(res)
    
    lists = ans

return list[0]

def insert(head, data)
    node = Node(data)
    node.next = head
    return node ^wemwjBHn

def ise(head, data):
    node = Node(data)
    if head is None:
        return node
    
    temp = head
    while temp.next is not None:
        temp = temp.next
    
    temp.next = node
    return head
     ^JYslrfev

fun iap(head, data, position)
node = Node(data)
if position = 0:
    node.next = head
    return node

temp = head
for i in range(position -1 )
    if temp is None:
        return head
    temp = temp.next

node.next = temp.next
temp.next = node
return head ^FmGKsNjw

def dfb(head):
    if head is None:
        return None
    
    return head.next ^bXqLKMz7

def dfe(head):
    if head is none or head.next is none
        rturn none
    
    temp = head
    while temp.next.next
        temp = temp.next

    temp.next = none
return head
     ^Q75BIDLF

def dfp(head, pos)

if head is none:
    return none

if pos  == 0
    return head.next

temp = head
for i in range(pos -1)
    if temp is none
        return head
    temp = temp.next

if temp.next:
    tenp.next = temp.next.next
